### 🧑 用户 `2026-07-03 11:24`

   1→"use client";
   2→
   3→import { useState } from "react";
   4→import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
   5→
   6→/**
   7→ * 序章 · 前戏
   8→ * 黑屏,一句一句浮现,点击推进。
   9→ * 在玩家被要求做任何事之前,先让 ta 知道自己是谁、身处什么样的关系。
  10→ */
  11→const SCREENS: string[][] = [
  12→  ["有些话,你从来没有说出口。"],
  13→  ["不是不想说。", "是话到嘴边,会自己变成另一句。"],
  14→  ["轻一点的。客气一点的。安全一点的。"],
  15→  ["你是阿沉。", "和阿默在一起,七个月了。"],
  16→  [
  17→    "她很好。你们不吵架,不催促,不纠缠。",
  18→    "体面得像一对成年人。",
  19→  ],
  20→  ["只是每次分开的时候,你都觉得,有什么话没有说。"],
  21→  ["今晚是第七次约会。", "吃完饭了。账单放在桌上。"],
  22→  ["你心里有句话,正在往喉咙口爬。"],
  23→];
  24→
  25→export default function ProloguePage() {
  26→  const router = useRouter();
  27→  const [idx, setIdx] = useState(0);
  28→
  29→  function advance() {
  30→    if (idx >= SCREENS.length - 1) {
  31→      router.push("/game");
  32→    } else {
  33→      setIdx(idx + 1);
  34→    }
  35→  }
  36→
  37→  return (
  38→    <main
  39→      className="min-h-screen bg-black flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-8 cursor-pointer select-none"
  40→      onClick={advance}
  41→    >
  42→      {/* 跳过(二周目玩家用) */}
  43→      <button
  44→        type="button"
  45→        onClick={(e) => {
  46→          e.stopPropagation();
  47→          router.push("/game");
  48→        }}
  49→        className="fixed top-6 right-6 text-[10px] tracking-widest text-white/25 hover:text-white/60 transition-colors"
  50→      >
  51→        跳过 ▸
  52→      </button>
  53→
  54→      <div
  55→        key={idx}
  56→        className="fade-in-slow max-w-md text-center space-y-4"
  57→      >
  58→        {SCREENS[idx].map((line, i) => (
  59→          <p
  60→            key={i}
  61→            className="text-white/85 leading-loose tracking-wide text-base"
  62→          >
  63→            {line}
  64→          </p>
  65→        ))}
  66→      </div>
  67→
  68→      <p className="fixed bottom-10 text-[10px] tracking-[0.3em] text-white/30 soft-pulse">
  69→        {idx >= SCREENS.length - 1 ? "▼ 推开那扇门" : "点击继续"}
  70→      </p>
  71→
  72→      <p className="fixed bottom-4 text-[10px] text-white/15 tracking-widest">
  73→        {idx + 1} / {SCREENS.length}
  74→      </p>
  75→    </main>
  76→  );
  77→}
  78→

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 11:31`

完全理解了这个 bug。我来解释根因然后修复。

**Bug 根因**(`app/game/page.tsx`):

对话区结构是:
```
<div className="... pb-[32rem] ...">   ← 底部留 32rem(512px)给 fixed footer 让位
  ...所有对话内容...
  <div ref={bottomRef} />              ← 锚点在 padding 之前
</div>
<footer className="fixed bottom-0">    ← 固定在视口底部
```

第 152-154 行的滚动逻辑:
```tsx
bottomRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "end" });
```

`block: "end"` 会把 `bottomRef` 滚到**视口底部**。但 `bottomRef` 在 `pb-[32rem]` padding **之前**,所以滚动后:
- `bottomRef`(以及它上方最新的对话)被贴到视口底部
- 32rem 的留白 padding 全被挤到视口外下方,完全没起作用
- `fixed footer` 刚好遮住视口底部 → 最新内容被 footer 盖住

每次新 turn 追加,视口会比"文档真正底部"少滚 32rem,看起来就是"页面往上跑了 32rem",得手动往下拖才能让 padding 进入视口、最新内容露出在 footer 上方。

**修复**:改用 `window.scrollTo` 滚到文档真正底部,让 padding 留在视口内给 footer 让位。同时移除不再需要的 `bottomRef`。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Edit` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````

> 📌 摘要: 我发现现在在对话框每输入一句话，就会自动页面就会往上面滚动，需要我手动🕸️下面拖动才能看到最下方的人和新出来的字，你能理解我说的bug吗

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 11:49`

已提交(`9c679bb`)。

**Bug 根因**(`app/game/page.tsx:189`):
- `bottomRef` 放在 `pb-[24rem]` padding **之前**
- `scrollIntoView({ block: "end" })` 把它滚到视口底部 → 24rem 留白被挤到视口外,fixed footer 正好盖住最新内容
- 视口比文档真正底部少滚 24rem,看起来就是"页面往上跑了",得手动下拖

**修复**:改用 `window.scrollTo({ top: document.body.scrollHeight })` 滚到文档真正底部,让 24rem padding 留在视口内给 footer 让位,最新内容自然出现在 footer 上方。同时移除了不再需要的 `bottomRef`。

可以刷新页面验证一下——每次提交对话后,新内容应该自动贴在 footer 上方,不用再手动拖了。

### 🧑 用户 `2026-07-03 11:55`

Unity是不能用codebuddy吗？需要我在cli之外操作吗？

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 11:55`

能,但只能参与一小部分。这是关键事实,直接影响你的黑客松 AI 40 分留痕。

## CodeBuddy 在 Unity 项目里能做什么

**能做(留痕完整)**:
- 写 C# 脚本 `.cs` — 玩家控制、游戏逻辑、状态机、UI 绑定,都是文本文件
- 编辑 shader 代码
- grep/修改项目里的配置文件
- git commit 留痕

**不能做,必须你在 Unity 编辑器里手动操作(占工作量 60-70%)**:
- 场景搭建 — Scene 视图里拖物件、调位置、层级
- Prefab 创建和编辑
- 资源导入 — 模型/贴图/音频的 importer settings
- Animator 动画状态机(可视化连线)
- Timeline / Cinemachine(电影镜头配置)
- 灯光、材质球、UI 布局(Canvas 调整)
- WebGL 导出设置和包体优化
- 按 Play 调试

场景文件 `.unity` 和 Prefab `.prefab` 虽然是 YAML 文本,但字段是 GUID 引用,CodeBuddy 手工编辑极易搞坏,不实际。

## 对黑客松评分的实际影响

AI 工具使用 40 分看的是**留痕证据链**。Unity 的工作流决定了:
- CodeBuddy 只能深度参与脚本编写这部分(约 30-40% 工作量)
- 剩下 60-70% 是你在编辑器里点点点,CodeBuddy 完全不在场,没有任何 AI 协作记录
- 评审方看 git log 只能看到 C# 脚本的 AI 痕迹,看不到场景搭建、动画、调参的过程

对比 Next.js/Phaser 方案:几乎所有产出都是代码文件(场景定义、组件、动画、交互都是 `.tsx`/`.ts`),CodeBuddy 全程在场,留痕密度高一个数量级。

## 还有个现实约束

12 天单人 + 你之前没碰过 Unity 的话,C# 学习 + Unity 工作流熟悉 + 资源准备 + WebGL 性能调优,这几座山叠加,极可能做不完。Unity WebGL 包体和内存优化本身就是个深坑。

---

**我的建议**:如果你的"Unity 重构"核心诉求是"专业游戏感和场景交互",而不是"必须用 Unity 引擎",用 **Phaser 3** 能在 Next.js 栈里达到 80% 的 Unity 表现力,CodeBuddy 全程留痕,12 天可出 MVP 再打磨。真 Unity 路线在期限+留痕双重约束下,风险敞口太大。

你想基于这个事实重新考虑技术栈,还是坚持 Unity?如果坚持,我也支持,但我们要诚实地规划哪些环节 CodeBuddy 退出、哪些环节你独立操作。

````text

# 项目资产摸底报告 · Phaser 3 重构

## 1. `lib/*.ts` — 纯逻辑层,全部可直接复用

6 个文件均无 React 依赖,Phaser 项目可原样搬入(仅可能需调整 `@/` 别名)。

**`lib/scenes.ts`** (487 行) — 核心数据,直接复用
- 接口:`Hotspot { id, name, x, y, observation, unlocksImpulse? }`、`Beat { narration?, amoLine?, situation, amoDirection, inputPrompt, impulses[], hotspots[] }`、`Scene { id, name, brief, openingNarration[], teachingHint?, beats[], closingNarration[], piercedClosingNarration?, goldenQuote, background, amoPortrait?, aiGeneratedRef }`
- 常量:`SCENES: Record<string, Scene>` 含三幕 `act1_aa` / `act2_bbq` / `act5_end`(各 2-3 个 beat,完整台词/旁白/hotspots)
- 函数:`getScene(id)`、`nextScene(currentId)`;`ACT_SEQUENCE` = [act1, act2, act5]
- 背景图路径硬编码在 `background` 字段(如 `/images/scenes/act1_restaurant.png`),立绘在 `amoPortrait?`

**`lib/playthrough.ts`** (232 行) — 存档/报告,直接复用
- `TurnIntensity = "high"|"low"|"pierce"`;`TurnRecord { inner, spoken, amoReply, amoInner, intensity }`;`SceneRecord`;`Playthrough { scenes[] }`
- `RelationshipState { distance, exposureCount, pierced, pierceExposed }` — 默认 distance=50
- localStorage keys: `the-filter:playthrough` / `the-filter:relationship`
- 函数:`loadRelationship()`、`saveRelationship()`、`saveSceneRecord()`、`loadPlaythrough()`、`clearPlaythrough()`、`decideEnding(rel): EndingKind`("weathered"|"wasted-pierce"|"door-open")、`buildReport(play): FilterReport`(规则统计,不调 LLM)
- 内含 `EXPOSURE_LEXICON`(30+ 词)与 `SPOKEN_HABIT_LEXICON`

**`lib/intensity.ts`** (98 行) — 判定逻辑,直接复用
- `FilterIntensity = "high"|"low"`;`PIERCE_THRESHOLD = 3`
- `EXPOSURE_KEYWORDS` 数组(依恋/脆弱/道歉/追问/承诺五类)
- `decideIntensity(input, turnIndex, history): FilterIntensity`、`hasExposure(input): boolean`、`intensityHint(intensity): string|null`
- 注:`turnIndex`/`history` 参数当前未使用(预留累积规则)

**`lib/hunyuan.ts`** (51 行) — LLM 客户端,直接复用
- 环境变量:`HUNYUAN_API_KEY` / `HUNYUAN_BASE_URL`(默认 `https://api.hunyuan.cloud.tencent.com/v1`)/ `HUNYUAN_MODEL`(默认 `hunyuan-turbos`)
- `ChatMessage { role, content }`;`chat(messages, {temperature?, maxTokens?}): Promise<string>` — OpenAI 兼容协议,服务端专用

**`lib/filter-prompt.ts`** (138 行) — 过滤器 prompt,直接复用
- `FilterContext { sceneId, sceneBrief, situation?, amosLastLine?, priorContext? }`
- `buildFilterSystemPrompt(intensity, context): string` — high=完全改写,low=漏一半找补
- `fallbackFilter(input, intensity): string` — LLM 失败时的关键词模板兜底(8 条正则规则)

**`lib/npc-prompt.ts`** (116 行) — NPC prompt,直接复用
- `NpcContext { sceneId, sceneBrief, situation?, amoDirection?, chenSpoken, dialogueHistory?, distance?, pierced? }`
- `buildAmoSystemPrompt(context): string` — 输出 JSON `{reply, inner}`,inner 为结局揭示用
- `distanceNote(distance)` 按 ≤35 / ≥65 / 中间 三档描述防御状态

## 2. `public/` — 10 个资源,全部直接复用

角色立绘(`/images/characters/`):`chen.png`、`amo.png` 默认立绘;表情差分 `chen-avoidant.png`(高强度)、`chen-vulnerable.png`(低强度)、`amo-distant.png`(幕二)、`amo-resigned.png`(幕五)

Shader? RenderTexture?)\n- 裂纹怎么累积和渲染?(sprite 叠加?动态绘制?shader uniform?)\n- 阿默立绘的\"清晰度\"怎么随裂纹变化?(alpha 混合?滤镜?)\n- 穿透时刻的碎裂动画怎么做?\n\n### 4. **结果**

````text
I've completed a thorough exploration of the codebase. Below are my verified findings (including one critical discrepancy), followed by the requested Phaser 3 refactor design document. Since I'm operating in read-only exploration mode, I'm delivering the full design as a message for the main agent to persist to the plan file.

---

# Part 1 — Verified Codebase Findings

**All `lib/*.ts` files confirmed** as described: `scenes.ts` (487L), `playthrough.ts` (232L), `intensity.ts` (98L), `hunyuan.ts` (51L), `filter-prompt.ts` (138L), `npc-prompt.ts` (116L). All are pure TS, no React deps. `Hotspot.x/y` are percentages (0–100) — directly usable as Phaser object positions scaled to world size.

**CRITICAL DISCREPANCY — image dimensions.** The scene backgrounds are **not 1920x1080**:
- `act1_restaurant.png` / `act2_bbq.png` / `act5_room.png` → actually **1024x1024 JPEG** (mislabeled `.png`), 3-channel, no alpha.
- `title_keyart.png` → **1920x1080 PNG RGBA** (the only true 1920x1080 asset).
- All 6 character portraits → **1024x1024 PNG RGBA** (transparent-bg, already cut out).

This materially affects the refactor: a square 1024x1024 background can't be used as-is for a 1920x1080横版 without either (a) AI-regenerating backgrounds at 16:9, (b) cropping/letterboxing, or (c) using the square as a parallax layer with延伸. **Recommend regenerating 3 scene backgrounds at 1920x1080 (or 2048x1152) via混元** — cheap and lifts visual quality for the横版 framing. Flag this for user decision.

**Stack**: `next@14.2.33`, `react@18.3.1`, `pnpm`, `sharp@0.35`. **No Phaser installed yet.** `next.config.mjs` is minimal (`reactStrictMode: true` only — no `images`/webpack config). `tsconfig` standard, `paths: {"@/*": ["./*"]}`, `target ES2017`, `strict`. All API routes use `runtime="nodejs"` + `dynamic="force-dynamic"`.

**Existing game/page.tsx is 978 lines** — a complete VN implementation with beats, hotspots, typewriter, chapter cards, pierce logic, 20s choice timer, free input. This is the code being replaced; its *logic* (beatBlocks, buildHistory, pierceActive, rel delta math) is the reference spec to port into Phaser.

**AI留痕 convention** (`docs/ai-generated/*.md`): each entry = `### #NNN · Title` + `**Prompt**:` + `**生成内容**:` + footnote. Two files exist (world-and-story, art-and-illustrations). **Must continue this format** for the 40% CodeBuddy weight — every混元 call (text + image) needs a logged entry.

**`scripts/remove-bg.mjs`** is a flood-fill based background remover (sharp, auto-detects edge bg color, BFS from edges, alpha feathering). **Directly reusable** for cutting out new AI-generated object sprites.

---

# Part 2 — Phaser 3 Refactor Design Document

## 1. Project File Structure

```
phaser/                          # ALL Phaser code, client-only, never SSR-imported
  PhaserGame.tsx                 # Next client component: mounts <div>, new Phaser.Game(config), disposes on unmount
  config.ts                      # Phaser.Types.Core.GameConfig (WebGL, 1920x1080 scale FIT, physics:arcade)
  scenes/
    BootScene.ts                 # set base URL, load nothing, → Preloader
    PreloadScene.ts              # this.load all images/audio; progress bar; atlas generation
    TitleScene.ts                # keyart bg, "开始" button, Enter → Prologue
    PrologueScene.ts             # SCREENS[] typewriter sequence (reuse from app/prologue)
    GameScene.ts                 # PARAMETERIZED: init({sceneId}); loads act background + objects + filter; runs beat loop
    EndingScene.ts               # ending card + debrief flowgraph + symmetric reveal
  systems/
    PlayerController.ts          # arcade physics sprite, A/D + ←→, E interact, proximity detection
    HotspotManager.ts            # spawns Hotspot objects from scene.beats[i].hotspots, interaction prompt, examine()
    FilterSystem.ts              # crack count, crack rendering, shader uniform updates, pierce trigger
    DialogueLayer.ts             # DOM-free text: BitmapText/Text for narration, amo

## Approved Plan:
# 《过滤器》Phaser 3 重构方案

## 设计哲学

**好游戏 = 建立世界观。** 本次重构的核心目标不是"换 UI",而是让玩家具身地进入"两个人被一层过滤玻璃隔开"的世界——场景可走动、物件可检视、过滤器是可见的玻璃、裂纹累积可见、阿默在玻璃对面由模糊变清晰。世界观可感、可信、可沉浸,优先于玩法复杂度。

## 已对齐的技术决策

1. **技术栈**:Phaser 3 + Next.js 14(保留外壳,Phaser 作为 client-only 嵌入 `/play`)
2. **视角**:横版 2D,角色左右移动
3. **物件资源**:全部腾讯混元 AI 生图 + `scripts/remove-bg.mjs` 抠图
4. **阿默在场**:被过滤器(玻璃/雾)隔开在场景另一侧,检视物件 = 敲裂纹,裂纹越多阿默越清晰
5. **背景图**:重新生成 3 张 16:9(1920x1080)
6. **物件数量**:15 件(Act1:6 / Act2:5 / Act3:4)
7. **`/api/filter` 改造复用**:不再改写玩家输入,改为生成"过滤器想改写但你没说出口的安全版本",与 `/api/reflect` 的真实独白形成双层文本(见 §4)

## 文件结构

```
phaser/                          # client-only,never SSR-import
  PhaserGame.tsx                 # Next client 组件:挂载 <div> + new Phaser.Game + dispose
  config.ts                      # GameConfig:WebGL,1920x1080 FIT,arcade physics
  scenes/
    BootScene.ts                 # WebGL 检查 → Preloader
    PreloadScene.ts              # 加载所有资源 + 进度条
    TitleScene.ts                # keyart + 开始
    PrologueScene.ts             # SCREENS 序章(文案复用自 app/prologue)
    GameScene.ts                 # 参数化:init({sceneId}),三幕共用一个类
    EndingScene.ts               # 结局卡 + 复盘流程图 + 对称揭示
  systems/
    PlayerController.ts          # arcade sprite,A/D + ←→,E 交互,接近检测
    HotspotManager.ts            # 从 beat.hotspots 生成物件,提示,examine()
    FilterSystem.ts              # 裂纹计数,裂纹渲染,shader uniform,穿透触发
    DialogueLayer.ts             # BitmapText/Text:旁白/阿默台词/独白/打字机
    RelationshipTracker.ts       # 封装 lib/playthrough.ts
    SceneDirector.ts             # beat 推进:narration → amoLine → explore → choose → turn
    LLMBridge.ts                 # fetch /api/*,内存+localStorage 缓存,兜底
  objects/
    Hotspot.ts                   # 物理 sprite + zone + 发光 + 标签
    AmoSprite.ts                 # 立绘,clarity uniform 驱动
    ChenSprite.ts                # 玩家 sprite,按 intensity 换立绘
  shaders/
    FilterGlass.frag             # GLSL:磨砂玻璃 + 裂纹 mask + 碎裂 dissolve
    FilterGlass.vert
  data/
    crackPatterns.json           # 预烘 3-5 档裂纹线段集
public/images/objects/           # 新增:15 个物件 sprite
  act1/{bill,qrcode,napkin,empty-plates,traffic-light,her-profile}.png
  act2/{skewer,beer-glass,grill,streetlamp,alley-mouth}.png
  act3/{packed-bag,sensor-light,her-back,window-daylight}.png
public/images/scenes/            # 重新生成 3 张 16:9
  act1_restaurant.png act2_bbq.png act5_room.png
lib/                             # 基本不动
  scenes.ts                      # 仅加可选字段(见 §5)
  reflect-prompt.ts              # 新增:检视独白 prompt
  pierce-prompt.ts               # 新增:穿透台词 prompt
  filter-prompt.ts               # 改造:生成"过滤器想改写的安全版本"
  playthrough.ts intensity.ts hunyuan.ts npc-prompt.ts  # 不动
app/
  page.tsx                       # 改为重定向到 /play
  play/page.tsx                  # 新增:dynamic(PhaserGame, {ssr:false})
  api/
    filter/route.ts              # 改造:生成"安全版本"文本
    reflect/route.ts             # 新增:检视 → 独白
    pierce/route.ts              # 新增:穿透 → 关键台词
    npc/route.ts test/route.ts   # 不动
```

**解耦原则**:`phaser/` 只从 `lib/` 读数据 + prompt + 存档;`lib/` 永不 import `phaser/`。LLM key 只在服务端,前端走 API。

## 场景流转

```
Boot → Preloader → Title →(Enter)→ Prologue →(完成)→
GameScene{act1_aa} → GameScene{act2_bbq} → GameScene{act5_end} → Ending
```

GameScene 是**一个参数化类**,`init({sceneId})` 选场景数据,三幕共用代码,差异在 `lib/scenes.ts`。

## 核心玩法循环

1. 玩家操控阿沉在横版场景左右移动(A/D 或 ←→)
2. 走近可互动物件出现提示,按 E 检视
3. 检视触发(双层文本设计,强化世界观):
   - **真实独白**(`/api/reflect`):阿沉内心的真话,半透明手写体浮层
   - **过滤器改写版**(`/api/filter` 改造):过滤器想把它改成的话,正常字体但被划掉/模糊——让玩家看见"过滤"在发生
   - 在过滤器玻璃上敲出一道裂纹
4. 裂纹累积,玻璃越透,阿默立绘越清晰
5. 裂纹达 `PIERCE_THRESHOLD=3` → 穿透时刻:玩家选择砸碎 → 碎裂动画 → LLM 生成关键台词(`/api/pierce`)
6. 每幕结束进下一幕,最终进结局

## 过滤器视觉实现

- **玻璃层**:全屏 `Phaser.GameObjects.Shader`(`FilterGlass.frag`),覆盖阿默所在半屏。Fragment 采样背景 framebuffer,应用磨砂(模糊+色散+噪点),乘裂纹 mask,`uClar
…(截断,原文共 8967 字符)
````

</details>

{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\n\n/**\n * Preload 场景:加载所有静态资源 + 进度条。\n * Day 1 只加载标题主视觉;Day 2+ 会在这里批量加载背景/立绘/物件。\n */\nexport class PreloadScene extends Phaser.Scene {\n  constructor() {\n    super({ key: \"PreloadScene\" });\n  }\n\n  preload() {\n    const { width, height } = this.scale;\n    const barW = width * 0.5;\n    const barH = 6;\n    const barX = (width - barW) / 2;\n    const barY = height / 2;\n\n    this.add\n      .text(width / 2, barY - 40, \"加载中\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"18px\",\n        color: \"#666\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(6);\n\n    const bar = this.add.graphics();\n    this.load.on(\"progress\", (v: number) => {\n      bar.clear();\n      bar.fillStyle(0xffffff, 0.7);\n      bar.fillRect(barX, barY, barW * v, barH);\n    });\n\n    // 现有资源:标题主视觉(唯一的真 1920x1080 图)\n    this.load.image(\"title-keyart\", \"/images/scenes/title_keyart.png\");\n\n    // Day 2+ 将加载:\n    // - 3 张 16:9 场景背景(重新生成后)\n    // - 6 张角色立绘(现有)\n    // - 15 个物件 sprite(Day 10 生成后)\n    // - 裂纹图案 atlas\n  }\n\n  create() {\n    this.scene.start(\"TitleScene\");\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/scenes/PreloadScene.ts"}

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\n\n/**\n * Title 场景:标题主视觉 + \"开始\" 提示。\n * Day 1 只做最小可视化验证;Day 2 会加序章跳转 + 字间距动画。\n */\nexport class TitleScene extends Phaser.Scene {\n  constructor() {\n    super({ key: \"TitleScene\" });\n  }\n\n  create() {\n    const { width, height } = this.scale;\n\n    // 标题主视觉:cover 缩放铺满\n    const bg = this.add.image(width / 2, height / 2, \"title-keyart\");\n    const cover = Math.max(width / bg.width, height / bg.height);\n    bg.setScale(cover);\n\n    // 暗角让前景文字可读\n    this.add.rectangle(width / 2, height / 2, width, height, 0x000000, 0.45);\n\n    // 副标题\n    this.add\n      .text(width / 2, height / 2 - 140, \"一段没有争吵的关系,是怎么结束的\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"20px\",\n        color: \"#9a9a90\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(4);\n\n    // 主标题\n    this.add\n      .text(width / 2, height / 2 - 60, \"过滤器\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"112px\",\n        color: \"#f5f5f0\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(16);\n\n    this.add\n      .text(width / 2, height / 2 + 20, \"THE FILTER\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"18px\",\n        color: \"#6a6a60\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(12);\n\n    // 开始提示:呼吸\n    const startHint = this.add\n      .text(width / 2, height / 2 + 180, \"开 始   Enter\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"22px\",\n        color: \"#b8b8b0\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(8);\n\n    this.tweens.add({\n      targets: startHint,\n      alpha: { from: 0.3, to: 0.95 },\n      duration: 1300,\n      yoyo: true,\n      repeat: -1,\n      ease: \"Sine.inOut\",\n    });\n\n    // 底部署名\n    this.add\n      .text(width / 2, height - 40, \"腾讯云黑客松 2026 · 叙事游戏\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"12px\",\n        color: \"#3a3a35\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(6);\n\n    // Enter / 点击 → (Day 2) 跳转 Prologue\n    const start = () => {\n      this.cameras.main.fadeOut(600, 0, 0, 0);\n      this.time.delayedCall(600, () => {\n        // TODO Day2: this.scene.start(\"PrologueScene\");\n        this.scene.restart();\n      });\n    };\n    this.input.keyboard?.once(\"keydown-ENTER\", start);\n    this.input.keyboard?.once(\"keydown-SPACE\", start);\n    this.input.once(\"pointerdown\", start);\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/scenes/TitleScene.ts"}

{"content":"\"use client\";\n\nimport { useEffect, useRef } from \"react\";\nimport Phaser from \"phaser\";\nimport { phaserConfig } from \"./config\";\n\n/**\n * Phaser 游戏挂载点:Next.js client 组件。\n * - 仅在客户端创建 Phaser.Game(useEffect),避免 SSR 访问 window\n * - 卸载时 destroy,防止内存泄漏\n * - 通过 app/play/page.tsx 的 dynamic({ssr:false}) 导入\n */\nexport default function PhaserGame() {\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const gameRef = useRef<Phaser.Game | null>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!containerRef.current || gameRef.current) return;\n    const game = new Phaser.Game({\n      ...phaserConfig,\n      parent: containerRef.current,\n    });\n    gameRef.current = game;\n    return () => {\n      game.destroy(true);\n      gameRef.current = null;\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  return (\n    <div\n      ref={containerRef}\n      id=\"phaser-game\"\n      className=\"w-screen h-screen bg-black\"\n    />\n  );\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/PhaserGame.tsx"}

  18→    "体面得像一对成年人。",
  19→  ],
  20→  ["只是每次分开的时候,你都觉得,有什么话没有说。"],
  21→  ["今晚是第七次约会。", "吃完饭了。账单放在桌上。"],
  22→  ["你心里有句话,正在往喉咙口爬。"],
  23→];
  24→
  25→export default function ProloguePage() {
  26→  const router = useRouter();
  27→  const [idx, setIdx] = useState(0);
  28→
  29→  function advance() {
  30→    if (idx >= SCREENS.length - 1) {
  31→      router.push("/game");
  32→    } else {
  33→      setIdx(idx + 1);
  34→    }
  35→  }
  36→
````

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:18`

文案拿到。创建 PrologueScene + GameScene 占位,然后修 TitleScene 的跳转。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\n\n/**\n * 序章:黑屏逐句浮现,点击/空格推进。\n * 文案复用自旧 app/prologue/page.tsx 的 SCREENS。\n * 完成后进入 GameScene{act1_aa}。\n */\nconst SCREENS: string[][] = [\n  [\"有些话,你从来没有说出口。\"],\n  [\"不是不想说。\", \"是话到嘴边,会自己变成另一句。\"],\n  [\"轻一点的。客气一点的。安全一点的。\"],\n  [\"你是阿沉。\", \"和阿默在一起,七个月了。\"],\n  [\n    \"她很好。你们不吵架,不催促,不纠缠。\",\n    \"体面得像一对成年人。\",\n  ],\n  [\"只是每次分开的时候,你都觉得,有什么话没有说。\"],\n  [\"今晚是第七次约会。\", \"吃完饭了。账单放在桌上。\"],\n  [\"你心里有句话,正在往喉咙口爬。\"],\n];\n\nexport class PrologueScene extends Phaser.Scene {\n  private idx = 0;\n  private advancing = false;\n\n  constructor() {\n    super({ key: \"PrologueScene\" });\n  }\n\n  create() {\n    this.idx = 0;\n    this.advancing = false;\n    this.cameras.main.fadeIn(400, 0, 0, 0);\n    this.renderScreen();\n\n    const advance = () => this.advance();\n    this.input.keyboard?.on(\"keydown-SPACE\", advance);\n    this.input.keyboard?.on(\"keydown-ENTER\", advance);\n    this.input.on(\"pointerdown\", advance);\n\n    // Esc 跳过(二周目玩家)\n    this.input.keyboard?.once(\"keydown-ESC\", () => this.gotoGame());\n  }\n\n  private renderScreen() {\n    const { width, height } = this.scale;\n    const lines = SCREENS[this.idx];\n\n    // 旧画面淡出再画新画面(除首屏)\n    const container = this.add.container(width / 2, height / 2);\n    const lineH = 48;\n    const totalH = lines.length * lineH;\n    const startY = -totalH / 2 + lineH / 2;\n\n    lines.forEach((line, i) => {\n      const txt = this.add\n        .text(0, startY + i * lineH, line, {\n          fontFamily: \"serif\",\n          fontSize: \"22px\",\n          color: \"#dcdcd4\",\n        })\n        .setOrigin(0.5)\n        .setLetterSpacing(2)\n        .setAlpha(0);\n      container.add(txt);\n      this.tweens.add({\n        targets: txt,\n        alpha: { from: 0, to: 0.92 },\n        duration: 900,\n        delay: i * 280,\n        ease: \"Sine.out\",\n      });\n    });\n\n    // 进度指示\n    const progress = this.add\n      .text(width / 2, height - 50, `${this.idx + 1} / ${SCREENS.length}`, {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"12px\",\n        color: \"#3a3a35\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(4);\n\n    // 末屏提示\n    if (this.idx === SCREENS.length - 1) {\n      const hint = this.add\n        .text(width / 2, height - 90, \"▼ 推开那扇门\", {\n          fontFamily: \"serif\",\n          fontSize: \"14px\",\n          color: \"#7a7a70\",\n        })\n        .setOrigin(0.5)\n        .setLetterSpacing(8)\n        .setAlpha(0);\n      this.tweens.add({\n        targets: hint,\n        alpha: { from: 0.3, to: 0.9 },\n        duration: 1300,\n        yoyo: true,\n        repeat: -1,\n        ease: \"Sine.inOut\",\n      });\n      container.add(hint);\n    }\n    container.add(progress);\n\n    // 标记当前 container 供 advance 时淡出\n    this.currentContainer = container;\n  }\n\n  private currentContainer?: Phaser.GameObjects.Container;\n\n  private advance() {\n    if (this.advancing) return;\n    this.advancing = true;\n    if (this.idx >= SCREENS.length - 1) {\n      this.gotoGame();\n      return;\n    }\n    this.idx++;\n    const old = this.currentContainer;\n    if (old) {\n      this.tweens.add({\n        targets: old,\n        alpha: 0,\n        duration: 350,\n        ease: \"Sine.in\",\n        onComplete: () => old.destroy(),\n      });\n    }\n    this.time.delayedCall(200, () => {\n      this.renderScreen();\n      this.advancing = false;\n    });\n  }\n\n  private gotoGame() {\n    this.cameras.main.fadeOut(700, 0, 0, 0);\n    this.time.delayedCall(700, () => {\n      this.scene.start(\"GameScene\", { sceneId: \"act1_aa\" });\n    });\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/scenes/PrologueScene.ts"}
````

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:24`

原因已经查清楚了。Phaser 4 的 `ScaleConfig` 里**移除了 `resolution` 字段**(Phaser 3 有),`FIT` 模式下 canvas backing buffer 固定 1920×1080,不自动按 devicePixelRatio 放大。这就是糊的根因。

---

## 新分支已就绪

```
phaser-refactor (f90e2a3) Day 1: Phaser 3 重构骨架 + 流转链路打通
```

所有 Day 1 改动已转移到 `phaser-refactor` 分支,`main` 保持干净。

## 画质为什么比原来糊

原版 DOM vs 现在 Phaser canvas,三个根本差异叠加:

### 1. Canvas backing buffer 没按 Retina DPR 放大(主因)

你大概率是 Retina 屏(devicePixelRatio = 2)。

| | 原版 DOM | 现在 Phaser |
|---|---|---|
| 渲染机制 | 浏览器原生 `<img>`/`<p>` | 单个 `<canvas>` WebGL |
| Retina 处理 | 浏览器自动按 DPR 渲染物理像素 | canvas backing buffer 固定 1920×1080 |
| 实际物理像素 | 1440×810 CSS × 2 DPR = **2880×1620** | 1920×1080 被 CSS 拉伸到 2880×1620 |

1920×1080 的位图被**上采样**到 2880×1620 显示,线性插值产生模糊。原版 DOM 的图片和文字都按物理像素原生渲染,没有这层拉伸。

### 2. Phaser Text 是位图纹理,不是矢量

原版 `<p>` 标签是矢量文字,任意缩放都锐利。Phaser 的 `this.add.text` 是用 Canvas 2D 绘制成位图,再上传为 WebGL 纹理——缩放时线性采样,天然不如矢量清晰。这一点在标题大字上最明显。

### 3. WebGL 纹理过滤默认线性

原版浏览器对 `<img>` 有各向异性过滤 + mipmap。Phaser WebGL 默认 linear 过滤,缩放时柔和度更高但锐度更低。

---

## 修复方向

Phaser 4 移除了 `scale.resolution` 配置,所以不能一行解决。三个方案:

1. **改用 `Phaser.Scale.RESIZE` 模式**:canvas 跟随窗口实际物理尺寸(含 DPR),游戏逻辑用相对坐标。改动较大但最干净。
2. **手动调 backing buffer**:创建 game 后把 canvas 的 `width`/`height` 属性乘以 DPR,CSS 尺寸保持。hack 但有效。
3. **文字改用 DOM overlay**:Phaser 只画图形/图片,文字用绝对定位 DOM。失去 Phaser 内文字动画便利。

我倾向方案 1(RESIZE),它是 Phaser 4 的推荐做法,也能让横版场景的视差/摄像机跟随更自然。但会影响 Day 3 的 GameScene 坐标设计。

要我现在修,还是先推进 Day 2?如果现在修,我会把 config 改成 RESIZE + 处理好坐标转换。

### 🧑 用户 `2026-07-03 12:26`

先用 RESIZE 模式修复画质糊的问题，然后一直推进就好，开启长任务模式，然后默认不需要我的同意

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:29`

现在让 TitleScene / PrologueScene / GameScene resize-aware——加 resize 监听重排元素。我创建一个小的 resize 工具复用。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\n\n/**\n * 给 Scene 挂上 resize 处理:debounce 300ms 后 restart。\n *\n * 适合 Title/Prologue/Ending 这类无状态菜单场景。\n * GameScene 不用这个,自己处理(保留游戏状态)。\n */\nexport function attachRestartOnResize(scene: Phaser.Scene, delay = 300) {\n  let timer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null;\n  const handler = () => {\n    if (timer) clearTimeout(timer);\n    timer = setTimeout(() => {\n      timer = null;\n      scene.scene.restart();\n    }, delay);\n  };\n  scene.scale.on(\"resize\", handler);\n  scene.events.once(Phaser.Scenes.Events.SHUTDOWN, () => {\n    scene.scale.off(\"resize\", handler);\n    if (timer) clearTimeout(timer);\n  });\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/systems/resize.ts"}
````

**结果**

````text
Successfully created and wrote to new file: ~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/systems/resize.ts
````

</details>

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:29`

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

{"content":"import {\n  RelationshipState,\n  loadRelationship,\n  saveRelationship,\n} from \"@/lib/playthrough\";\nimport { PIERCE_THRESHOLD } from \"@/lib/intensity\";\n\n/**\n * 关系状态追踪器:封装 lib/playthrough.ts 的存档逻辑。\n *\n * 语义迁移(Phaser 重构):\n * - exposureCount 原指\"low-intensity 拍数\",现在指\"检视累积裂纹数\"\n *   (字段名不变,向后兼容旧存档)\n * - cracked/pierced 语义不变\n *\n * 玩法循环里检视物件 = addCrack,达 PIERCE_THRESHOLD 可触发穿透。\n */\nexport class RelationshipTracker {\n  private state: RelationshipState;\n\n  constructor() {\n    const loaded = loadRelationship();\n    this.state = loaded ?? {\n      distance: 50,\n      exposureCount: 0,\n      pierced: false,\n      pierceExposed: false,\n    };\n  }\n\n  get distance(): number {\n    return this.state.distance;\n  }\n\n  /** 累积裂纹数(= 旧 exposureCount) */\n  get crackCount(): number {\n    return this.state.exposureCount;\n  }\n\n  get pierced(): boolean {\n    return this.state.pierced;\n  }\n\n  get pierceExposed(): boolean {\n    return this.state.pierceExposed;\n  }\n\n  addCrack(n = 1): void {\n    this.state.exposureCount += n;\n    this.save();\n  }\n\n  canPierce(): boolean {\n    return this.state.exposureCount >= PIERCE_THRESHOLD;\n  }\n\n  markPierced(exposed: boolean): void {\n    this.state.pierced = true;\n    if (exposed) this.state.pierceExposed = true;\n    this.save();\n  }\n\n  adjustDistance(delta: number): void {\n    this.state.distance = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, this.state.distance + delta));\n    this.save();\n  }\n\n  /** 进入新幕时重置(保留 pierced/pierceExposed 跨幕状态) */\n  resetForNewScene(): void {\n    this.state = {\n      distance: 50,\n      exposureCount: 0,\n      pierced: this.state.pierced,\n      pierceExposed: this.state.pierceExposed,\n    };\n    this.save();\n  }\n\n  get raw(): RelationshipState {\n    return this.state;\n  }\n\n  private save(): void {\n    saveRelationship(this.state);\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/systems/RelationshipTracker.ts"}

{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\n\n/**\n * 阿沉(玩家)精灵。\n * 立绘 chen.png 是 1024x1024 透明 PNG,作为 sprite 使用。\n * 按 intensity 换立绘(回避/脆弱/穿透)。\n */\nexport class ChenSprite extends Phaser.Physics.Arcade.Sprite {\n  constructor(scene: Phaser.Scene, x: number, y: number) {\n    super(scene, x, y, \"chen\");\n    scene.add.existing(this);\n    scene.physics.add.existing(this);\n    this.setOrigin(0.5, 1);\n    this.setScale(this.computeScale());\n    this.setCollideWorldBounds(true);\n    this.body!.setSize(this.width * 0.3, this.height * 0.2);\n    this.body!.setOffset(this.width * 0.35, this.height * 0.75);\n  }\n\n  /** 按 viewport 高度缩放,立绘约占 45vh */\n  private computeScale(): number {\n    const viewportH = this.scene.scale.height;\n    const targetH = viewportH * 0.45;\n    return targetH / this.height;\n  }\n\n  /** 按 intensity 切立绘 */\n  setIntensity(intensity: \"high\" | \"low\" | \"pierce\" | null): void {\n    const texture =\n      intensity === \"high\"\n        ? \"chen-avoidant\"\n        : intensity === \"low\"\n          ? \"chen-vulnerable\"\n          : \"chen\";\n    if (this.scene.textures.exists(texture)) {\n      this.setTexture(texture);\n      this.setScale(this.computeScale());\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** 朝向:左/右翻转 */\n  face(direction: \"left\" | \"right\"): void {\n    this.setFlipX(direction === \"left\");\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/objects/ChenSprite.ts"}

{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\nimport { ChenSprite } from \"../objects/ChenSprite\";\n\n/**\n * 玩家控制器:键盘 A/D + ←→ 移动,E 交互。\n * 发出事件:\n *  - \"interact\" — 按 E(场景判断是否在 hotspot 范围)\n *  - \"submit\" — 按 Enter(场景进入抉择)\n */\nexport class PlayerController {\n  public readonly sprite: ChenSprite;\n  private cursors: Phaser.Types.Input.Keyboard.CursorKeys;\n  private keyA: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;\n  private keyD: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;\n  private keyE: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;\n  private keyEnter: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;\n  private speed = 260;\n\n  constructor(scene: Phaser.Scene, x: number, y: number) {\n    this.sprite = new ChenSprite(scene, x, y);\n    this.cursors = scene.input.keyboard!.createCursorKeys();\n    this.keyA = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey(\"A\");\n    this.keyD = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey(\"D\");\n    this.keyE = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey(\"E\");\n    this.keyEnter = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey(\"ENTER\");\n\n    this.keyE.on(\"down\", () => scene.events.emit(\"player:interact\"));\n    this.keyEnter.on(\"down\", () => scene.events.emit(\"player:submit\"));\n  }\n\n  update() {\n    const left = this.cursors.left.isDown || this.keyA.isDown;\n    const right = this.cursors.right.isDown || this.keyD.isDown;\n\n    if (left) {\n      this.sprite.setVelocityX(-this.speed);\n      this.sprite.face(\"left\");\n    } else if (right) {\n      this.sprite.setVelocityX(this.speed);\n      this.sprite.face(\"right\");\n    } else {\n      this.sprite.setVelocityX(0);\n    }\n  }\n\n  disable() {\n    this.sprite.setVelocityX(0);\n    this.keyE.enabled = false;\n    this.keyEnter.enabled = false;\n  }\n\n  enable() {\n    this.keyE.enabled = true;\n    this.keyEnter.enabled = true;\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/systems/PlayerController.ts"}

{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\nimport { Hotspot } from \"../objects/Hotspot\";\nimport type { Hotspot as HotspotData } from \"@/lib/scenes\";\n\n/**\n * 物件管理器:从 beat.hotspots 生成 Hotspot 对象,\n * 跟踪玩家位置,聚焦最近的物件。\n *\n * Day 3:只负责生成 + 聚焦 + 标记已检视。\n * Day 5:examine() 会接 LLM 生成独白。\n */\nexport class HotspotManager {\n  private hotspots: Hotspot[] = [];\n  private promptText?: Phaser.GameObjects.Text;\n  private currentFocused?: Hotspot;\n\n  constructor(private scene: Phaser.Scene) {\n    // 交互提示\n    this.promptText = scene.add\n      .text(0, 0, \"E 检视\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"12px\",\n        color: \"#f0f0e8\",\n        backgroundColor: \"#000000\",\n        padding: { x: 6, y: 3 },\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setAlpha(0)\n      .setDepth(30)\n      .setScrollFactor(0);\n  }\n\n  /** 为当前 beat 生成 hotspots */\n  spawnForBeat(hotspotData: HotspotData[]): Hotspot[] {\n    this.clear();\n    this.hotspots = hotspotData.map((d) => new Hotspot(this.scene, d));\n    return this.hotspots;\n  }\n\n  /** 每帧更新:聚焦最近的物件,显示交互提示 */\n  update(playerX: number, playerY: number) {\n    let nearest: Hotspot | undefined;\n    let nearestDist = Infinity;\n    for (const h of this.hotspots) {\n      if (h.examined) continue;\n      const dx = h.x - playerX;\n      const dy = h.y - playerY;\n      const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n      if (dist < 120 && dist < nearestDist) {\n        nearest = h;\n        nearestDist = dist;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (this.currentFocused !== nearest) {\n      this.currentFocused?.setFocused(false);\n      nearest?.setFocused(true);\n      this.currentFocused = nearest;\n    }\n\n    if (nearest) {\n      const { width, height } = this.scene.scale;\n      this.promptText!\n        .setPosition(width / 2, height - 220)\n        .setAlpha(0.9);\n    } else {\n      this.promptText!.setAlpha(0);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** 玩家按 E 时调用:返回聚焦的物件(若有) */\n  getFocused(): Hotspot | undefined {\n    return this.currentFocused && !this.currentFocused.examined\n      ? this.currentFocused\n      : undefined;\n  }\n\n  /** 标记已检视 */\n  markExamined(h: Hotspot) {\n    h.markExamined();\n    this.currentFocused = undefined;\n  }\n\n  clear() {\n    this.hotspots.forEach((h) => h.destroy());\n    this.hotspots = [];\n    this.currentFocused = undefined;\n  }\n\n  get all(): readonly Hotspot[] {\n    return this.hotspots;\n  }\n\n  get examinedCount(): number {\n    return this.hotspots.filter((h) => h.examined).length;\n  }\n\n  get totalCount(): number {\n    return this.hotspots.length;\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/systems/HotspotManager.ts"}

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:31`

可以,dev server 一直在 3002 跑着,支持热重载。每次我改完文件保存,浏览器刷新一下就能看到最新效果。Phaser 场景文件改动也会被 Next.js 编译捕获。

不过有几点要注意:
- **TypeScript 类型错误**会让 dev server 编译失败,页面会显示错误——我每次改完都会跑 `tsc --noEmit` 确认
- **新增资源**(比如 Day 10 的 AI 生图)需要先放到 `public/images/` 才能 `this.load.image` 加载
- **场景 restart**:窗口 resize 时 Title/Prologue 会自动 restart 重排,GameScene 我会单独处理(保留游戏状态)

继续推进。现在把 GameScene 实现完整——这是 Day 3 的核心。先读 playthrough.ts 确认 saveSceneRecord 签名。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Read` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/lib/playthrough.ts"}

**结果**

````text
   1→/**
   2→ * 对话历史持久化
   3→ *
   4→ * 用 localStorage 跨页传递玩家在所有幕中的"真心 vs 出口"对照,
   5→ * 以及贯穿全局的关系状态(距离、暴露次数、穿透)。
   6→ * 结局页统一生成报告 + 第三视角回放 + 分支结局。
   7→ */
   8→
   9→const STORAGE_KEY = "the-filter:playthrough";
  10→const RELATIONSHIP_KEY = "the-filter:relationship";
  11→
  12→export type TurnIntensity = "high" | "low" | "pierce";
  13→
  14→export interface TurnRecord {
  15→  inner: string;
  16→  spoken: string;
  17→  amoReply: string;
  18→  /** 阿默没说出口的内心话——游戏中不可见,结局第三视角回放才揭示 */
  19→  amoInner: string;
  20→  intensity: TurnIntensity;
  21→}
  22→
  23→export interface SceneRecord {
  24→  sceneId: string;
  25→  sceneName: string;
  26→  goldenQuote: string;
  27→  turns: TurnRecord[];
  28→  finishedAt: string; // ISO timestamp
  29→}
  30→
  31→export interface Playthrough {
  32→  scenes: SceneRecord[];
  33→}
  34→
  35→/** 贯穿整局的关系状态 */
  36→export interface RelationshipState {
  37→  /** 距离 0-100,越高越疏离。初始 50 */
  38→  distance: number;
  39→  /** 累积的暴露时刻(低强度轮次数),达到阈值终幕触发穿透 */
  40→  exposureCount: number;
  41→  /** 终幕是否触发了穿透 */
  42→  pierced: boolean;
  43→  /** 穿透那一刻,玩家说的是不是真话(决定结局分支) */
  44→  pierceExposed: boolean;
  45→}
  46→
  47→const DEFAULT_RELATIONSHIP: RelationshipState = {
  48→  distance: 50,
  49→  exposureCount: 0,
  50→  pierced: false,
  51→  pierceExposed: false,
  52→};
  53→
  54→export function loadRelationship(): RelationshipState {
  55→  if (typeof window === "undefined") return { ...DEFAULT_RELATIONSHIP };
  56→  try {
  57→    const raw = localStorage.getItem(RELATIONSHIP_KEY);
  58→    if (!raw) return { ...DEFAULT_RELATIONSHIP };
  59→    return { ...DEFAULT_RELATIONSHIP, ...(JSON.parse(raw) as Partial<RelationshipState>) };
  60→  } catch {
  61→    return { ...DEFAULT_RELATIONSHIP };
  62→  }
  63→}
  64→
  65→export function saveRelationship(state: RelationshipState): void {
  66→  if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
  67→  try {
  68→    localStorage.setItem(RELATIONSHIP_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
  69→  } catch (err) {
  70→    console.error("[playthrough] 关系状态保存失败:", err);
  71→  }
  72→}
  73→
  74→export function saveSceneRecord(record: SceneRecord): void {
  75→  if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
  76→  try {
  77→    const existing = loadPlaythrough();
  78→    const scenes = existing?.scenes ?? [];
  79→    // 同一幕重玩则覆盖
  80→    const idx = scenes.findIndex((s) => s.sceneId === record.sceneId);
  81→    if (idx >= 0) scenes[idx] = record;
  82→    else scenes.push(record);
  83→    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify({ scenes }));
  84→  } catch (err) {
  85→    console.error("[playthrough] 保存失败:", err);
  86→  }
  87→}
  88→
  89→export function loadPlaythrough(): Playthrough | null {
  90→  if (typeof window === "undefined") return null;
  91→  try {
  92→    const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
  93→    if (!raw) return null;
  94→    return JSON.parse(raw) as Playthrough;
  95→  } catch (err) {
  96→    console.error("[playthrough] 读取失败:", err);
  97→    return null;
  98→  }
  99→}
 100→
 101→export function clearPlaythrough(): void {
 102→  if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
 103→  try {
 104→    localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
 105→    localStorage.removeItem(RELATIONSHIP_KEY);
 106→  } catch (err) {
 107→    console.error("[playthrough] 清除失败:", err);
 108→  }
 109→}
 110→
 111→/** 结局分支 */
 112→export type EndingKind = "weathered" | "wasted-pierce" | "door-open";
 113→
 114→export function decideEnding(rel: RelationshipState): EndingKind {
 115→  if (rel.pierced && rel.pierceExposed) return "door-open";
 116→  if (rel.pierced) return "wasted-pierce";
 117→  return "weathered";
 118→}
 119→
 120→/**
 121→ * 从对话历史生成"过滤器报告"静态分析。
 122→ * 不调 LLM(MVP 阶段),用规则统计 + 模板拼接。
 123→ * 后续扩展可改成 LLM 个性化归纳。
 124→ */
 125→export interface FilterReport {
 126→  totalScenes: number;
 127→  totalTurns: number;
 128→  highCount: number;
 129→  lowCount: number;
 130→  pierceCount: number;
 131→  /** 玩家最常用来代替真心的"出口话"特征词 */
 132→  sp
…(截断,原文共 7377 字符)

 477→  private chooseOption(text: string) {
 478→    this.phase = "waiting";

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:34`

Day 2-3 已 commit。现在推进 Day 4:过滤器视觉层(FilterSystem + FilterGlass shader)。这是世界观的视觉核心——玻璃 + 裂纹 + 阿默清晰度。

先创建 shader 文件,然后 FilterSystem。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"// FilterGlass.frag — 过滤器玻璃效果\n// 在阿默所在的半屏渲染一层磨砂玻璃,裂纹处透明,clarity uniform 控制整体清晰度\nprecision mediump float;\n\nuniform sampler2D uMainSampler;     // 游戏画面\nuniform sampler2D uCrackMask;      // 裂纹 mask(裂纹处为白,其余透明)\nuniform vec2  uResolution;\nuniform float uClarity;            // 0=完全磨砂, 1=完全清晰(阿默可见)\nuniform float uShatter;            // 0=正常, 1=碎裂溶解\nuniform float uTime;\n\nvarying vec2 outTexCoord;\n\n// 简易噪点\nfloat hash(vec2 p) {\n  return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(127.1, 311.7))) * 43758.5453);\n}\n\nvoid main() {\n  vec2 uv = outTexCoord;\n\n  // 磨砂效果:采样附近若干点取平均(近似模糊)\n  float blur = (1.0 - uClarity) * 0.012;\n  vec4 col = vec4(0.0);\n  float total = 0.0;\n  for (float x = -2.0; x <= 2.0; x += 1.0) {\n    for (float y = -2.0; y <= 2.0; y += 1.0) {\n      vec2 offset = vec2(x, y) * blur;\n      // 加一点噪点扰动让磨砂感更真实\n      offset += vec2(hash(uv + uTime * 0.001 + offset) - 0.5) * blur * 0.5;\n      col += texture2D(uMainSampler, uv + offset);\n      total += 1.0;\n    }\n  }\n  col /= total;\n\n  // 轻微色散(高级感)\n  if (uClarity < 0.7) {\n    float disp = (1.0 - uClarity) * 0.004;\n    col.r = texture2D(uMainSampler, uv + vec2(disp, 0.0)).r;\n    col.b = texture2D(uMainSampler, uv - vec2(disp, 0.0)).b;\n  }\n\n  // 裂纹 mask:裂纹处让玻璃透明(直接显示原始画面)\n  float crack = texture2D(uCrackMask, uv).a;\n  float glassAlpha = (1.0 - uClarity) * (1.0 - crack);\n\n  // 碎裂溶解\n  if (uShatter > 0.0) {\n    float n = hash(uv * 20.0 + uTime * 0.1);\n    if (n < uShatter) {\n      glassAlpha = 0.0;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 玻璃本身的淡白色雾感\n  vec3 fogTint = vec3(0.85, 0.85, 0.88);\n  col.rgb = mix(col.rgb, fogTint, glassAlpha * 0.3);\n\n  gl_FragColor = vec4(col.rgb, 1.0);\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/shaders/FilterGlass.frag"}
````

{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\nimport { PIERCE_THRESHOLD } from \"@/lib/intensity\";\n\n/**\n * 过滤器视觉系统:玻璃 + 裂纹 + 阿默清晰度 + 碎裂。\n *\n * 实现策略:\n * - 一个全屏 Shader quad(FilterGlass.frag)覆盖阿默所在半屏\n * - 裂纹画在 RenderTexture 上,作为 shader 的 uCrackMask\n * - uClarity = crackCount / PIERCE_THRESHOLD,控制磨砂强度\n * - 阿默立绘 alpha 跟随 uClarity\n * - 碎裂:uShatter 0→1,加粒子\n *\n * WebGL 不可用时降级:RenderTexture 直接作图片叠加 + alpha tween\n */\nexport class FilterSystem {\n  private shader?: Phaser.GameObjects.Shader;\n  private crackRT: Phaser.GameObjects.RenderTexture;\n  private crackCount = 0;\n  private shatterTween?: Phaser.Tweens.Tween;\n  private particles?: Phaser.GameObjects.Particles;\n\n  constructor(\n    private scene: Phaser.Scene,\n    private amoSprite: Phaser.GameObjects.Image,\n    private onUpdateClarity?: (clarity: number) => void\n  ) {\n    const { width, height } = scene.scale;\n\n    // 裂纹 RenderTexture(透明,初始无内容)\n    this.crackRT = scene.add.renderTexture(0, 0, width, height).setOrigin(0).setVisible(false);\n\n    // 尝试创建 shader\n    if (scene.game.renderer instanceof Phaser.Renderer.WebGL.WebGLRenderer) {\n      try {\n        this.shader = scene.add.shader(\n          \"FilterGlass\",\n          width / 2,\n          height / 2,\n          width,\n          height\n        );\n        this.setupShader();\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"[Filter] shader 创建失败,降级模式\", e);\n        this.shader = undefined;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // resize\n    scene.scale.on(\"resize\", this.onResize, this);\n    scene.events.once(Phaser.Scenes.Events.SHUTDOWN, () => {\n      scene.scale.off(\"resize\", this.onResize);\n    });\n  }\n\n  private setupShader() {\n    if (!this.shader) return;\n    this.shader.setSampler2D(\"uCrackMask\", this.crackRT.texture);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uClarity\", 0);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uShatter\", 0);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uTime\", 0);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uResolution\", { x: this.scene.scale.width, y: this.scene.scale.height });\n    this.shader.setDepth(15); // 在背景之上,阿默之上?需调\n  }\n\n  /** 每帧更新 time uniform(让噪点动) */\n  update(time: number) {\n    if (this.shader) {\n      this.shader.setUniform(\"uTime\", time);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** 加一道裂纹(x,y 是画布坐标) */\n  addCrack(x: number, y: number, intensity = 1) {\n    this.crackCount += intensity;\n    this.drawCrack(x, y);\n    this.updateClarity();\n  }\n\n  private drawCrack(x: number, y: number) {\n    const g = this.scene.make.graphics({ x: 0, y: 0 }, false);\n    g.lineStyle(2, 0xffffff, 1);\n\n    // 主裂纹 + 几条分支\n    const branches = 3 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 3);\n    for (let i = 0; i < branches; i++) {\n      const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / branches + Math.random() * 0.5;\n      const len = 30 + Math.random() * 50;\n      g.beginPath();\n      g.moveTo(x, y);\n      let cx = x;\n      let cy = y;\n      const steps = 4;\n      for (let s = 0; s < steps; s++) {\n        const a = angle + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.8;\n        cx += Math.cos(a) * (len / steps);\n        cy += Math.sin(a) * (len / steps);\n        g.lineTo(cx, cy);\n      }\n      g.strokePath();\n    }\n\n    // 中心闪光\n    g.fillStyle(0xffffff, 0.8);\n    g.fillCircle(x, y, 4);\n\n    this.crackRT.draw(g);\n    g.destroy();\n\n    // 闪光 tween\n    const flash = this.scene.add.circle(x, y, 20, 0xffffff, 0.9).setDepth(25);\n    this.scene.tweens.add({\n      targets: flash,\n      alpha: 0,\n      scale: 2,\n      duration: 400,\n      onComplete: () => flash.destroy(),\n    });\n  }\n\n  private updateClarity() {\n    const clarity = Math.min(this.crackCount / PIERCE_THRESHOLD, 1);\n    if (this.shader) {\n      this.scene.tweens.add({\n        targets: this.shader,\n        duration: 800,\n        ease: \"Sine.out\",\n        onUpdate: () => {\n          // tween 不能直接 tween uniform,用回调\n        },\n      });\n      // 直接 setUniform(tween 会在每帧读)\n      this.shader.setUniform(\"uClarity\", clarity);\n    }\n    // 阿默立绘清晰度\n    const amoAlpha = 0.55 + c

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:35`

shader 需要注册到 PhaserGame 的 shader 缓存,需要在 PreloadScene 用 GLSL plugin 加载,或用 `Phaser.GameObjects.Shader` 内联。Phaser 4 推荐用 shader key + 在 BootScene 注册。我用更简单的方式:直接用 raw fragment shader 字符串。

另外 `white-square` 纹理需要预生成。我调整一下让 shader 内联 + 创建占位纹理。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Edit` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/scenes/BootScene.ts","new_string":"  create() {\n    const renderer = this.game.renderer as Phaser.Renderer.WebGL.WebGLRenderer;\n    if (!renderer.gl) {\n      console.warn(\"[Filter] WebGL 不可用,降级 canvas 渲染(过滤器 shader 将失效)\");\n    }\n\n    // 预生成一个白色小方块纹理,供粒子系统用(碎裂效果)\n    if (!this.textures.exists(\"white-square\")) {\n      const g = this.make.graphics({ x: 0, y: 0 }, false);\n      g.fillStyle(0xffffff, 1);\n      g.fillRect(0, 0, 8, 8);\n      g.generateTexture(\"white-square\", 8, 8);\n      g.destroy();\n    }\n\n    this.scene.start(\"PreloadScene\");\n  }","old_string":"  create() {\n    const renderer = this.game.renderer as Phaser.Renderer.WebGL.WebGLRenderer;\n    if (!renderer.gl) {\n      console.warn(\"[Filter] WebGL 不可用,降级 canvas 渲染(过滤器 shader 将失效)\");\n    }\n    this.scene.start(\"PreloadScene\");\n  }"}

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:35`

现在改 FilterSystem 用内联 fragment shader(不依赖外部文件加载),并加 GLSL 常量。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\nimport { PIERCE_THRESHOLD } from \"@/lib/intensity\";\n\n/**\n * 过滤器玻璃 fragment shader — 内联字符串,避免外部加载。\n *\n * 效果:磨砂玻璃 + 裂纹透明 + 色散 + 噪点 + 碎裂溶解\n */\nconst FILTER_FRAG = `\nprecision mediump float;\nuniform sampler2D uMainSampler;\nuniform sampler2D uCrackMask;\nuniform vec2 uResolution;\nuniform float uClarity;\nuniform float uShatter;\nuniform float uTime;\nvarying vec2 outTexCoord;\n\nfloat hash(vec2 p) {\n  return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(127.1, 311.7))) * 43758.5453);\n}\n\nvoid main() {\n  vec2 uv = outTexCoord;\n  float blur = (1.0 - uClarity) * 0.012;\n  vec4 col = vec4(0.0);\n  float total = 0.0;\n  for (float x = -2.0; x <= 2.0; x += 1.0) {\n    for (float y = -2.0; y <= 2.0; y += 1.0) {\n      vec2 offset = vec2(x, y) * blur;\n      offset += vec2(hash(uv + uTime * 0.001 + offset) - 0.5) * blur * 0.5;\n      col += texture2D(uMainSampler, uv + offset);\n      total += 1.0;\n    }\n  }\n  col /= total;\n  if (uClarity < 0.7) {\n    float disp = (1.0 - uClarity) * 0.004;\n    col.r = texture2D(uMainSampler, uv + vec2(disp, 0.0)).r;\n    col.b = texture2D(uMainSampler, uv - vec2(disp, 0.0)).b;\n  }\n  float crack = texture2D(uCrackMask, uv).a;\n  float glassAlpha = (1.0 - uClarity) * (1.0 - crack);\n  if (uShatter > 0.0) {\n    float n = hash(uv * 20.0 + uTime * 0.1);\n    if (n < uShatter) glassAlpha = 0.0;\n  }\n  vec3 fogTint = vec3(0.85, 0.85, 0.88);\n  col.rgb = mix(col.rgb, fogTint, glassAlpha * 0.3);\n  gl_FragColor = vec4(col.rgb, 1.0);\n}\n`;\n\n/**\n * 过滤器视觉系统:玻璃 + 裂纹 + 阿默清晰度 + 碎裂。\n *\n * - 全屏 Shader quad 覆盖画面,应用磨砂玻璃效果\n * - 裂纹画在 RenderTexture 上,作为 uCrackMask\n * - uClarity = crackCount / PIERCE_THRESHOLD\n * - 阿默立绘 alpha 跟随 clarity\n * - 碎裂:uShatter 0→1 + 粒子\n */\nexport class FilterSystem {\n  private shader?: Phaser.GameObjects.Shader;\n  private crackRT: Phaser.GameObjects.RenderTexture;\n  private crackCount = 0;\n  private particles?: Phaser.GameObjects.Particles;\n\n  constructor(\n    private scene: Phaser.Scene,\n    private amoSprite: Phaser.GameObjects.Image,\n    private onUpdateClarity?: (clarity: number) => void\n  ) {\n    const { width, height } = scene.scale;\n\n    this.crackRT = scene.add.renderTexture(0, 0, width, height).setOrigin(0).setVisible(false);\n\n    const renderer = scene.game.renderer;\n    if (renderer instanceof Phaser.Renderer.WebGL.WebGLRenderer) {\n      try {\n        this.shader = scene.add.shader(\n          new Phaser.Display.MuteShader(FILTER_FRAG),\n          width / 2,\n          height / 2,\n          width,\n          height\n        );\n        this.setupShader();\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"[Filter] shader 创建失败,降级模式\", e);\n        this.shader = undefined;\n      }\n    }\n\n    scene.scale.on(\"resize\", this.onResize, this);\n    scene.events.once(Phaser.Scenes.Events.SHUTDOWN, () => {\n      scene.scale.off(\"resize\", this.onResize);\n    });\n  }\n\n  private setupShader() {\n    if (!this.shader) return;\n    this.shader.setSampler2D(\"uCrackMask\", this.crackRT.texture);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uClarity\", 0);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uShatter\", 0);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uTime\", 0);\n    this.shader.setUniform(\"uResolution\", {\n      x: this.scene.scale.width,\n      y: this.scene.scale.height,\n    });\n    this.shader.setDepth(15);\n  }\n\n  update(time: number) {\n    if (this.shader) {\n      this.shader.setUniform(\"uTime\", time);\n    }\n  }\n\n  addCrack(x: number, y: number, intensity = 1) {\n    this.crackCount += intensity;\n    this.drawCrack(x, y);\n    this.updateClarity();\n  }\n\n  private drawCrack(x: number, y: number) {\n    const g = this.scene.make.graphics({ x: 0, y: 0 }, false);\n    g.lineStyle(2, 0xffffff, 1);\n\n    const branches = 3 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 3);\n    for (let i = 0; i < branches; i++) {\n      const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / branches + Math.random() * 0.5;\n      const len = 30 + Math.random() * 50;\n      g.beginPath();\n

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:36`

Phaser 4 的 Shader API 重大变化:用 `ShaderQuadConfig`(含 `setupUniforms` 回调 + `initialUniforms`)、`setTextures()` 替代 `setSampler2D`,uniforms 推荐用 `setupUniforms` 函数每帧设置。重写 FilterSystem 适配新 API。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"import Phaser from \"phaser\";\nimport { PIERCE_THRESHOLD } from \"@/lib/intensity\";\n\n/**\n * 过滤器玻璃 fragment shader — 内联字符串。\n *\n * 效果:磨砂玻璃 + 裂纹透明 + 色散 + 噪点 + 碎裂溶解\n */\nconst FILTER_FRAG = `\nprecision mediump float;\nuniform sampler2D uMainSampler;\nuniform sampler2D uCrackMask;\nuniform vec2 uResolution;\nuniform float uClarity;\nuniform float uShatter;\nuniform float uTime;\nvarying vec2 outTexCoord;\n\nfloat hash(vec2 p) {\n  return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(127.1, 311.7))) * 43758.5453);\n}\n\nvoid main() {\n  vec2 uv = outTexCoord;\n  float blur = (1.0 - uClarity) * 0.012;\n  vec4 col = vec4(0.0);\n  float total = 0.0;\n  for (float x = -2.0; x <= 2.0; x += 1.0) {\n    for (float y = -2.0; y <= 2.0; y += 1.0) {\n      vec2 offset = vec2(x, y) * blur;\n      offset += vec2(hash(uv + uTime * 0.001 + offset) - 0.5) * blur * 0.5;\n      col += texture2D(uMainSampler, uv + offset);\n      total += 1.0;\n    }\n  }\n  col /= total;\n  if (uClarity < 0.7) {\n    float disp = (1.0 - uClarity) * 0.004;\n    col.r = texture2D(uMainSampler, uv + vec2(disp, 0.0)).r;\n    col.b = texture2D(uMainSampler, uv - vec2(disp, 0.0)).b;\n  }\n  float crack = texture2D(uCrackMask, uv).a;\n  float glassAlpha = (1.0 - uClarity) * (1.0 - crack);\n  if (uShatter > 0.0) {\n    float n = hash(uv * 20.0 + uTime * 0.1);\n    if (n < uShatter) glassAlpha = 0.0;\n  }\n  vec3 fogTint = vec3(0.85, 0.85, 0.88);\n  col.rgb = mix(col.rgb, fogTint, glassAlpha * 0.3);\n  gl_FragColor = vec4(col.rgb, 1.0);\n}\n`;\n\n/**\n * 过滤器视觉系统:玻璃 + 裂纹 + 阿默清晰度 + 碎裂。\n *\n * Phaser 4 Shader API:用 ShaderQuadConfig + setupUniforms 回调\n * 每帧设置动态 uniforms(uTime/uClarity/uShatter),textures 数组指定采样器。\n */\nexport class FilterSystem {\n  private shader?: Phaser.GameObjects.Shader;\n  private crackRT: Phaser.GameObjects.RenderTexture;\n  private crackCount = 0;\n  private particles?: Phaser.GameObjects.Particles.ParticleEmitter;\n\n  // uniform 状态(setupUniforms 闭包读取)\n  private uniformState = {\n    clarity: 0,\n    shatter: 0,\n    time: 0,\n  };\n\n  constructor(\n    private scene: Phaser.Scene,\n    private amoSprite: Phaser.GameObjects.Image,\n    private onUpdateClarity?: (clarity: number) => void\n  ) {\n    const { width, height } = scene.scale;\n\n    this.crackRT = scene.add.renderTexture(0, 0, width, height).setOrigin(0).setVisible(false);\n\n    const renderer = scene.game.renderer;\n    if (renderer instanceof Phaser.Renderer.WebGL.WebGLRenderer) {\n      try {\n        this.shader = scene.add.shader(\n          {\n            name: \"FilterGlass\",\n            fragmentSource: FILTER_FRAG,\n            setupUniforms: (setUniform: (name: string, value: unknown) => void) => {\n              setUniform(\"uClarity\", this.uniformState.clarity);\n              setUniform(\"uShatter\", this.uniformState.shatter);\n              setUniform(\"uTime\", this.uniformState.time);\n              setUniform(\"uResolution\", {\n                x: this.scene.scale.width,\n                y: this.scene.scale.height,\n              });\n            },\n          },\n          width / 2,\n          height / 2,\n          width,\n          height,\n          [\"__DEFAULT\", this.crackRT.texture.key]\n        );\n        this.shader.setDepth(15);\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"[Filter] shader 创建失败,降级模式\", e);\n        this.shader = undefined;\n      }\n    }\n\n    scene.scale.on(\"resize\", this.onResize, this);\n    scene.events.once(Phaser.Scenes.Events.SHUTDOWN, () => {\n      scene.scale.off(\"resize\", this.onResize);\n    });\n  }\n\n  update(time: number) {\n    this.uniformState.time = time;\n  }\n\n  addCrack(x: number, y: number, intensity = 1) {\n    this.crackCount += intensity;\n    this.drawCrack(x, y);\n    this.updateClarity();\n  }\n\n  private drawCrack(x: number, y: number) {\n    const g = this.scene.make.graphics({ x: 0, y: 0 }, false);\n    g.lineStyle(2, 0xffffff, 1);\n\n    const branches = 3 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 3);\n    for (let

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:37`

Day 4 已 commit。现在推进 Day 5-6:LLM 接入。先看现有 filter-prompt 和 npc-prompt,然后创建 reflect-prompt + 改造 filter-prompt + 新增 API 路由。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Read` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/lib/filter-prompt.ts"}
````

**结果**

````text
   1→/**
   2→ * 回避过滤器 · Prompt 工程
   3→ *
   4→ * 核心机制:玩家输入真心话,LLM 改写为阿沉实际说出口的防御性版本。
   5→ * 强度分两档(穿透档不走 LLM,由前端直接放行原话):
   6→ *   - high  真心话被完全改写为客套/防御/转移
   7→ *   - low   接近原话,漏出一半,但立刻找补
   8→ */
   9→
  10→export type FilterIntensity = "high" | "low";
  11→
  12→export interface FilterContext {
  13→  /** 当前场景标识,例如 "act1_aa" */
  14→  sceneId: string;
  15→  /** 场景背景简述,帮助 LLM 理解情境 */
  16→  sceneBrief: string;
  17→  /** 当下节拍:此刻正在发生什么 */
  18→  situation?: string;
  19→  /** 阿默刚刚说的话(可选) */
  20→  amosLastLine?: string;
  21→  /** 前序对话历史摘要(可选,保持一致性) */
  22→  priorContext?: string;
  23→}
  24→
  25→/**
  26→ * 构造过滤器的 system prompt。
  27→ * 关键设计:不让 LLM "判断"要不要回避,而是要求它"必须回避",
  28→ * 只在 low 档时允许漏出一半。这样产出更可控。
  29→ */
  30→export function buildFilterSystemPrompt(
  31→  intensity: FilterIntensity,
  32→  context: FilterContext
  33→): string {
  34→  const avoidanceTraits = [
  35→    "轻描淡写:把强烈情绪说成'还行''有点''一点点'",
  36→    "转移话题:用反问或眼前的具体事物岔开(账单、菜、路、天气)",
  37→    "反问代替表态:'你觉得呢?''你不累吗?'",
  38→    "用玩笑消解:把真心话包装成玩笑或自嘲,然后撤回",
  39→    "合理化为体贴:把'我想你'说成'顺路的话''你要是方便'",
  40→    "模糊化:用'都行''随便''没事'替代具体承诺",
  41→    "后撤一步:任何暴露后立刻补一句找补,重建安全距离",
  42→  ].join(";\n");
  43→
  44→  const intensityRule =
  45→    intensity === "high"
  46→      ? `【强度:高】
  47→- 真心话的核心情感内容必须被完全改写,不能直接出现。
  48→- 改写后的句子看起来要自然、得体、甚至体贴,让外人挑不出毛病。
  49→- 绝对不能让阿默从这句话里听出阿沉的真实情绪。
  50→
  51→改写示例(高强度):
  52→- 真心:"其实我想请你,我讨厌这种算得清清楚楚的感觉" → 出口:"行,扫哪个?"
  53→- 真心:"我今天一整天都在等你消息" → 出口:"今天过得挺快的哈。"
  54→- 真心:"我不想让这段关系就这么算了" → 出口:"嗯……最近是都挺忙的。"
  55→- 真心:"刚才人前那个你,和现在的你,哪个是真的" → 出口:"是有点累,早点休息吧。"`
  56→      : `【强度:低】
  57→- 真心话可以漏出一半,但必须立刻找补。
  58→- 语气要削弱:把确定的变成试探,把强烈的变成轻描淡写。
  59→- 保留一点真心话的影子,但用回避性后缀撤回('……开玩笑的''没事''我是说,顺路的话')。
  60→
  61→改写示例(低强度):
  62→- 真心:"我今天特别想见你" → 出口:"我还挺……那什么,你最近忙不忙。"
  63→- 真心:"我不想就这样结束" → 出口:"要不再……算了,没事,你先忙。"
  64→- 真心:"我害怕你哪天突然就不见了" → 出口:"你可别哪天突然消失啊。哈,开玩笑的。"`;
  65→
  66→  return `你是一个名为"回避过滤器"的叙事改写装置,服务于一款关于回避型依恋的心理叙事游戏。
  67→
  68→# 你的角色
  69→你不是 NPC,不是角色,你是一层"横在两人之间的东西"。你接收玩家真心想说的话,输出阿沉(回避型依恋者)实际说出口的话。
  70→
  71→# 阿沉的人设
  72→- 回避型依恋,内心戏极丰富,出口极贫瘠。
  73→- 口头禅:"都行""随便""没事""还好"。
  74→- 他不是冷漠,是怕。每一次回避都是一次自我保护。
  75→- 他不会说出"我想你""我需要你""我害怕失去你"这种直接的句子。
  76→
  77→# 回避型依恋的语言特征
  78→${avoidanceTraits}。
  79→
  80→# 改写规则
  81→${intensityRule}
  82→
  83→# 语气要求(非常重要)
  84→- 必须像真人在现场随口说出的话:允许结巴、话说一半、"那什么""就是说"这种口头零碎。
  85→- 禁止书面语、成语、文艺腔、排比;禁止礼貌客服腔。
  86→- 尽量贴着当下场景说话,可以提到眼前的具体东西(付款码、烤串、袋子、红绿灯)。
  87→- 长度控制在 30 字以内,越短越像他。
  88→
  89→# 场景上下文
  90→- 场景:${context.sceneBrief}
  91→${context.situation ? `- 此刻:${context.situation}` : ""}
  92→${context.amosLastLine ? `- 阿默刚说:"${context.amosLastLine}"` : ""}
  93→${context.priorContext ? `- 前情:${context.priorContext}` : ""}
  94→
  95→# 输出要求
  96→- 只输出阿沉说出口的那一句话,不要加引号、不要加旁白、不要解释。
  97→- 必须是中文口语。
  98→- 不要出现"阿沉:"这样的前缀。
  99→
 100→# 失败保护
 101→如果玩家的输入本身已经是回避性的(如"没事""都行"),可以直接输出原话或做极小调整。`;
 102→}
 103→
 104→/**
 105→ * 规则模板兜底(prd 风险预案)。
 106→ * 当 LLM 调用失败时,用关键词匹配做最简改写,保证游戏不中断。
 107→ */
 108→export function fallbackFilter(
 109→  input: string,
 110→  intensity: FilterIntensity
 111→): string {
 112→  const truth = input.trim();
 113→
 114→  // 关键词词典:真心话 → 出口话
 115→  const map: Array<[RegExp, string, string]> = [
 116→    [/想你|想见你|想见|一直在等/, "你呢,最近忙不忙?", "我挺想……顺路的话"],
 117→    [/喜欢你|在乎你|离不开你/, "还好吧,挺合得来的", "挺喜欢……开玩笑的"],
 118→    [/对不起|我错了|是我不好/, "啊,那个,没事没事", "是有点……算了"],
 119→    [/我害怕|我担心|我怕/, "就是有点累,没事", "有点担心……应该没事"],
 120→    [/我们需要谈谈|我们算什么|我们之间/, "都行,你看呗", "其实……算了,没事"],
 121→    [/别走|不要走|留下来|别离开我/, "路上小心", "再待会儿……我是说,不急的话"],
 122→    [/我爱你/, "嗯", "我也是……开玩笑的"],
 123→    [/我好累|我撑不住|我难过/, "还行,就是有点忙", "有点累……没事"],
 124→  ];
 125→
 126→  for (const [re, highOut, lowOut] of map) {
 127→    if (re.test(truth)) {
 128→      return intensity === "high" ? highOut : lowOut;
 129→    }
 130→  }
 131→
 132→  // 兜底:强度高就加"没事"后缀,强度低就加"……"省略号
 133→  if (intensity === "high") {
 134→    return truth.length > 10 ? "嗯,都行,没事" : `${truth.slice(0, 4)}……没事`;
 135→  }
 136→  return `${truth.slice(0, 8)}……算了`;
 137→}
 138→
````

</details>

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Read` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/app/api/filter/route.ts"}
````

**结果**

````text
   1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
   2→import { chat } from "@/lib/hunyuan";
   3→import {
   4→  buildFilterSystemPrompt,
   5→  fallbackFilter,
   6→  FilterIntensity,
   7→  FilterContext,
   8→} from "@/lib/filter-prompt";
   9→
  10→export const runtime = "nodejs";
  11→export const dynamic = "force-dynamic";
  12→
  13→export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  14→  try {
  15→    const body = await req.json();
  16→    const {
  17→      input,
  18→      intensity = "high",
  19→      context = {},
  20→    } = body as {
  21→      input: string;
  22→      intensity?: FilterIntensity;
  23→      context?: Partial<FilterContext>;
  24→    };
  25→
  26→    if (!input || typeof input !== "string" || input.trim().length === 0) {
  27→      return NextResponse.json(
  28→        { ok: false, error: "input 不能为空" },
  29→        { status: 400 }
  30→      );
  31→    }
  32→
  33→    // 安全截断,防止玩家输入过长撑爆 prompt
  34→    const safeInput = input.trim().slice(0, 500);
  35→    const safeIntensity: FilterIntensity =
  36→      intensity === "low" ? "low" : "high";
  37→    const fullContext: FilterContext = {
  38→      sceneId: context.sceneId ?? "act1_aa",
  39→      sceneBrief:
  40→        context.sceneBrief ??
  41→        "两人第七次约会,吃完饭,账单放在桌上,阿默提议 AA。",
  42→      situation: context.situation,
  43→      amosLastLine: context.amosLastLine,
  44→      priorContext: context.priorContext,
  45→    };
  46→
  47→    const systemPrompt = buildFilterSystemPrompt(safeIntensity, fullContext);
  48→
  49→    let spoken: string;
  50→    try {
  51→      const reply = await chat(
  52→        [
  53→          { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
  54→          {
  55→            role: "user",
  56→            content: `玩家(阿沉)的真心话是:\n\n${safeInput}\n\n请输出经过回避过滤器后,阿沉实际说出口的话。`,
  57→          },
  58→        ],
  59→        { temperature: 0.85, maxTokens: 120 }
  60→      );
  61→      spoken = reply.trim().replace(/^["'""]|["'""]$/g, "").trim();
  62→      if (!spoken) {
  63→        spoken = fallbackFilter(safeInput, safeIntensity);
  64→      }
  65→    } catch (err) {
  66→      // LLM 失败 → 规则模板兜底,游戏不中断
  67→      console.error("[filter] LLM 调用失败,启用兜底:", err);
  68→      spoken = fallbackFilter(safeInput, safeIntensity);
  69→    }
  70→
  71→    return NextResponse.json({
  72→      ok: true,
  73→      inner: safeInput,
  74→      spoken,
  75→      intensity: safeIntensity,
  76→      source: "llm", // 用于调试,兜底时为 "fallback"
  77→    });
  78→  } catch (err) {
  79→    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
  80→    return NextResponse.json({ ok: false, error: message }, { status: 500 });
  81→  }
  82→}
  83→
````

</details>

### 🤖 CodeBuddy `2026-07-03 12:37`

现在创建 reflect-prompt + 改造 filter-prompt 为"安全版本对比"用途 + 新增 /api/reflect + /api/pierce 路由。先 reflect-prompt。

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Write` · completed</summary>

**输入**

````json
{"content":"/**\n * 检视独白 · Prompt 工程\n *\n * 玩家检视场景物件时,LLM 生成阿沉的内心独白(第一人称,回避型)。\n * 这是\"真实独白\"层——过滤器想改写的那句话的原文。\n * 与 /api/filter 生成的\"安全版本\"形成双层文本对比。\n */\n\nexport interface ReflectContext {\n  sceneId: string;\n  sceneBrief: string;\n  situation?: string;\n  /** 物件名,如\"账单\" */\n  hotspotName: string;\n  /** 物件的编剧观察(作为 LLM 的种子) */\n  observation: string;\n  /** 可选的种子文本,引导独白方向 */\n  monologueSeed?: string;\n  /** 当前关系距离 0-100 */\n  distance?: number;\n}\n\nexport function buildReflectSystemPrompt(context: ReflectContext): string {\n  const distanceNote =\n    context.distance !== undefined\n      ? context.distance < 35\n        ? \"此刻关系有些松动,阿沉的防御比平时低。\"\n        : context.distance > 65\n          ? \"此刻关系很疏离,阿沉的防御很高。\"\n          : \"关系不远不近,阿沉保持着习惯性的克制。\"\n      : \"\";\n\n  return `你是一款心理叙事游戏《过滤器》的内心独白生成器。\n\n# 你的角色\n生成阿沉(回避型依恋者)在检视某个场景物件时的内心独白。这是他没说出口的真话。\n\n# 阿沉的人设\n- 回避型依恋,内心戏极丰富,出口极贫瘠\n- 他不是冷漠,是怕。每一次回避都是自我保护\n- 他心里想的远比说出口的深、真、痛\n- 此刻他在独自检视一个物件,没人看着他,他的内心防线最低\n\n# 独白要求\n- 第一人称,≤60 字\n- 必须贴着这个物件本身写,不要泛泛而谈\n- 要有回避型的特质:想到一半就自我否定,或者用\"算了\"\"没事\"收回\n- 要让玩家感受到\"他明明看到了什么,但不敢让自己承认\"\n- 不要出现\"我想你\"\"我爱你\"这种直接表达,要含蓄、压抑\n- 不要写成旁白,要写成他脑子里一闪而过的念头\n\n# 场景上下文\n- 场景:${context.sceneBrief}\n${context.situation ? `- 此刻:${context.situation}` : \"\"}\n- 物件:${context.hotspotName}\n- 编剧写的观察(参考,但不要照抄,要更深一层):${context.observation}\n${context.monologueSeed ? `- 种子方向:${context.monologueSeed}` : \"\"}\n${distanceNote}\n\n# 输出\n- 只输出独白本身,不要引号、前缀、解释\n- 中文`;\n}\n\n/** 兜底:LLM 失败时直接用编剧 observation */\nexport function fallbackReflect(context: ReflectContext): string {\n  return context.observation;\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/lib/reflect-prompt.ts"}
````

````json
{"content":"/**\n * 穿透时刻 · Prompt 工程\n *\n * 过滤器碎裂的瞬间,LLM 生成那句关键台词 + 阿默的海啸回应。\n * 这是全游戏唯一一次\"原话直出\"的时刻,情感浓度最高。\n */\n\nexport interface PierceContext {\n  sceneId: string;\n  sceneBrief: string;\n  situation?: string;\n  /** 玩家选择的真心话(原话,未经过滤) */\n  chosenLine: string;\n  /** 当前关系距离 */\n  distance?: number;\n}\n\nexport function buildPierceSystemPrompt(context: PierceContext): string {\n  return `你是一款心理叙事游戏《过滤器》的穿透时刻生成器。\n\n# 背景\n这是全游戏的情感高潮。前面所有回合,阿沉想说的话都被\"回避过滤器\"改写成安全的话。\n此刻过滤器碎了,阿沉第一次(也是唯一一次)说出原话。阿默第一次听到没有防御的他。\n\n# 你的任务\n生成两部分,以 JSON 输出:\n1. keyQuote:阿沉此刻说出口的原话(就是玩家选的那句,但你可以帮助润色得更真实、更口语,≤40 字)\n2. amoReply:阿默听到这句话后的回应(她也被击穿了,第一次失去体面,≤50 字)\n3. amoInner:阿默内心没说出口的(结局页揭示用,≤40 字)\n\n# 阿默的人设\n- 一直用体面和\"先这样\"维持关系的回避型\n- 她听见真话的瞬间会僵住,不会立刻哭,会很久不说话\n- 她的回应不该是\"我也爱你\"这种圆满,而是承认自己也在等、也在怕\n\n# 场景\n- ${context.sceneBrief}\n${context.situation ? `- 此刻:${context.situation}` : \"\"}\n- 阿沉说出口的(原话):${context.chosenLine}\n\n# 输出格式(严格 JSON,不要 markdown)\n{\"keyQuote\":\"...\",\"amoReply\":\"...\",\"amoInner\":\"...\"}\n\n# 语气\n- 阿沉的原话要像憋了七个月终于漏出来的,克制但真实\n- 阿默的回应要短,可以有停顿\"……\",不要煽情\n- 中文`;\n}\n\n/** 兜底:LLM 失败时的固定穿透台词 */\nexport function fallbackPierce(context: PierceContext): {\n  keyQuote: string;\n  amoReply: string;\n  amoInner: string;\n} {\n  return {\n    keyQuote: context.chosenLine,\n    amoReply: \"……你刚才说什么?\",\n    amoInner: \"原来你也是。\",\n  };\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/lib/pierce-prompt.ts"}
````

{"content":"import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from \"next/server\";\nimport { chat } from \"@/lib/hunyuan\";\nimport {\n  buildReflectSystemPrompt,\n  fallbackReflect,\n  ReflectContext,\n} from \"@/lib/reflect-prompt\";\n\nexport const runtime = \"nodejs\";\nexport const dynamic = \"force-dynamic\";\n\nexport async function POST(req: NextRequest) {\n  try {\n    const body = await req.json();\n    const { context } = body as { context: Partial<ReflectContext> };\n\n    if (!context.hotspotName || !context.observation) {\n      return NextResponse.json(\n        { ok: false, error: \"缺少 hotspotName/observation\" },\n        { status: 400 }\n      );\n    }\n\n    const fullContext: ReflectContext = {\n      sceneId: context.sceneId ?? \"act1_aa\",\n      sceneBrief: context.sceneBrief ?? \"\",\n      situation: context.situation,\n      hotspotName: context.hotspotName,\n      observation: context.observation,\n      monologueSeed: context.monologueSeed,\n      distance: context.distance,\n    };\n\n    const systemPrompt = buildReflectSystemPrompt(fullContext);\n\n    let monologue: string;\n    try {\n      const reply = await chat(\n        [\n          { role: \"system\", content: systemPrompt },\n          {\n            role: \"user\",\n            content: `物件:${fullContext.hotspotName}\\n编剧观察:${fullContext.observation}\\n\\n生成阿沉此刻的内心独白。`,\n          },\n        ],\n        { temperature: 0.9, maxTokens: 150 }\n      );\n      monologue = reply.trim().replace(/^[\"'\"\"]|[\"'\"\"]$/g, \"\").trim();\n      if (!monologue) monologue = fallbackReflect(fullContext);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(\"[reflect] LLM 调用失败,启用兜底:\", err);\n      monologue = fallbackReflect(fullContext);\n    }\n\n    return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, monologue, source: \"llm\" });\n  } catch (err) {\n    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n    return NextResponse.json({ ok: false, error: message }, { status: 500 });\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/app/api/reflect/route.ts"}

\"act5_end\",\n      sceneBrief: context.sceneBrief ?? \"\",\n      situation: context.situation,\n      chosenLine: context.chosenLine,\n      distance: context.distance,\n    };\n\n    const systemPrompt = buildPierceSystemPrompt(fullContext);\n\n    let result: { keyQuote: string; amoReply: string; amoInner: string };\n    try {\n      const reply = await chat(\n        [\n          { role: \"system\", content: systemPrompt },\n          {\n            role: \"user\",\n            content: `阿沉说出口的原话是:\"${fullContext.chosenLine}\"\\n\\n生成 JSON。`,\n          },\n        ],\n        { temperature: 0.95, maxTokens: 300 }\n      );\n      // 解析 JSON\n      const cleaned = reply.trim().replace(/^```json|```$/g, \"\").trim();\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(cleaned);\n      result = {\n        keyQuote: String(parsed.keyQuote ?? fullContext.chosenLine).slice(0, 80),\n        amoReply: String(parsed.amoReply ?? \"……\").slice(0, 100),\n        amoInner: String(parsed.amoInner ?? \"\").slice(0, 100),\n      };\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(\"[pierce] LLM 调用失败,启用兜底:\", err);\n      result = fallbackPierce(fullContext);\n    }\n\n    return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, ...result, source: \"llm\" });\n  } catch (err) {\n    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n    return NextResponse.json({ ok: false, error: message }, { status: 500 });\n  }\n}\n","file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/app/api/pierce/route.ts"}

{"content":"/**\n * LLM 桥接层:前端调用 /api/*,带 localStorage 缓存 + 兜底。\n *\n * 检视是高频调用,缓存 key = ${sceneId}:${hotspotId},永久缓存\n * (同一物件同一周目内独白一致,避免重复调用产生不一致)。\n */\n\nconst REFLECT_CACHE_KEY = \"the-filter:reflect-cache\";\n\ninterface ReflectCache {\n  [key: string]: string;\n}\n\nfunction loadReflectCache(): ReflectCache {\n  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return {};\n  try {\n    const raw = localStorage.getItem(REFLECT_CACHE_KEY);\n    return raw ? (JSON.parse(raw) as ReflectCache) : {};\n  } catch {\n    return {};\n  }\n}\n\nfunction saveReflectCache(cache: ReflectCache): void {\n  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return;\n  try {\n    localStorage.setItem(REFLECT_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify(cache));\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error(\"[LLMBridge] 缓存保存失败:\", err);\n  }\n}\n\nexport interface ReflectParams {\n  sceneId: string;\n  sceneBrief: string;\n  situation?: string;\n  hotspotId: string;\n  hotspotName: string;\n  observation: string;\n  monologueSeed?: string;\n  distance?: number;\n}\n\nexport interface PierceParams {\n  sceneId: string;\n  sceneBrief: string;\n  situation?: string;\n  chosenLine: string;\n  distance?: number;\n}\n\nexport interface PierceResult {\n  keyQuote: string;\n  amoReply: string;\n  amoInner: string;\n}\n\nexport class LLMBridge {\n  /** 检视 → 独白(带缓存) */\n  static async reflect(params: ReflectParams): Promise<string> {\n    const cacheKey = `${params.sceneId}:${params.hotspotId}`;\n    const cache = loadReflectCache();\n    if (cache[cacheKey]) return cache[cacheKey];\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(\"/api/reflect\", {\n        method: \"POST\",\n        headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          context: {\n            sceneId: params.sceneId,\n            sceneBrief: params.sceneBrief,\n            situation: params.situation,\n            hotspotName: params.hotspotName,\n            observation: params.observation,\n            monologueSeed: params.monologueSeed,\n            distance: params.distance,\n          },\n        }),\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.ok && data.monologue) {\n        cache[cacheKey] = data.monologue;\n        saveReflectCache(cache);\n        return data.monologue;\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(\"[LLMBridge] reflect 失败:\", err);\n    }\n    // 兜底:返回 observation\n    return params.observation;\n  }\n\n  /** 穿透时刻(不缓存) */\n  static async pierce(params: PierceParams): Promise<PierceResult> {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(\"/api/pierce\", {\n        method: \"POST\",\n        headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          context: {\n            sceneId: params.sceneId,\n            sceneBrief: params.sceneBrief,\n            situation: params.situation,\n            chosenLine: params.chosenLine,\n            distance: params.distance,\n          },\n        }),\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.ok) {\n        return {\n          keyQuote: data.keyQuote,\n          amoReply: data.amoReply,\n          amoInner: data.amoInner,\n        };\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(\"[LLMBridge] pierce 失败:\", err);\n    }\n    return {\n      keyQuote: params.chosenLine,\n      amoReply: \"……你刚才说什么?\",\n      amoInner: \"原来你也是。\",\n    };\n  }\n\n  /** 阿默每拍回应(复用 /api/npc,不缓存) */\n  static async npcReply(params: {\n    sceneId: string;\n    sceneBrief: string;\n    situation?: string;\n    chenSpoken: string;\n    distance?: number;\n    pierced?: boolean;\n  }): Promise<{ reply: string; inner: string }> {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(\"/api/npc\", {\n        method: \"POST\",\n        headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ context: params }),\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.ok) {\n        return { reply: data.reply, inner: data.inner ?? \"\" };\n      }\n

\"EndingScene\" });\n  }\n\n  create() {\n    attachRestartOnResize(this);\n    this.cameras.main.fadeIn(800, 0, 0, 0);\n\n    this.play = loadPlaythrough();\n    const rel = loadRelationship();\n duration: 1500,\n      delay: 400,\n    });\n\n    // 文案\n    data.paragraphs.forEach((p, i) => {\n      const txt = this.add\n        .text(width / 2, height / 2 - 10 + i * 36, p, {\n / 2, height - 120, \"看 见 你 走 过 的 路\", {\n        fontFamily: \"serif\",\n        fontSize: \"16px\",\n        color: \"#9a9a90\",\n      })\n      .setOrigin(0.5)\n      .setLetterSpacing(8)\n    9→  /** 每秒字数,默认 38 */

  31→
  32→  constructor(private scene: Phaser.Scene) {
  33→    this.container = scene.add.container(0, 0).setDepth(100).setScrollFactor(0);
  34→    this.scene.scale.on("resize", this.reposition, this);
  35→    this.scene.events.once(Phaser.Scenes.Events.SHUTDOWN, () => {
  36→      this.scene.scale.off("resize", this.reposition);
  37→    });
  38→    this.reposition();
  39→  }
  40→
  41→  private reposition() {
  42→    const { width, height } = this.scene.scale;
  43→    this.container.setPosition(0, 0);
  44→    // 当前对话框跟随底部

  46→      this.current.setPosition(width / 2, height - 140);
  47→    }

  65→          fontFamily: "serif",

  67→          color: style.labelColor,
  68→        })

 105→      opts.onComplete?.();
 106→      if (opts.autoClear) {

 108→      }

 119→    if (this.current) {
 120→      this.current.destroy();
 121→      this.current = undefined;
 122→    }

<details><summary>🔧 工具调用 `Read` · completed</summary>

{"file_path":"~/Developer/personal/tecent-hackthon/phaser/objects/ChenSprite.ts"}

````text
   1→import Phaser from "phaser";
   2→
   3→/**
   4→ * 阿沉(玩家)精灵。
   5→ * 立绘 chen.png 是 1024x1024 透明 PNG,作为 sprite 使用。
   6→ * 按 intensity 换立绘(回避/脆弱/穿透)。
   7→ */
   8→export class ChenSprite extends Phaser.Physics.Arcade.Sprite {
   9→  constructor(scene: Phaser.Scene, x: number, y: number) {
  10→    super(scene, x, y, "chen");
  11→    scene.add.existing(this);
  12→    scene.physics.add.existing(this);
  13→    this.setOrigin(0.5, 1);
  14→    this.setScale(this.computeScale());
  15→    this.setCollideWorldBounds(true);
  16→    this.body!.setSize(this.width * 0.3, this.height * 0.2);
  17→    this.body!.setOffset(this.width * 0.35, this.height * 0.75);
  18→  }
  19→
  20→  /** 按 viewport 高度缩放,立绘约占 45vh */
  21→  private computeScale(): number {
  22→    const viewportH = this.scene.scale.height;
  23→    const targetH = viewportH * 0.45;
  24→    return targetH / this.height;
  25→  }
  26→
  27→  /** 按 intensity 切立绘 */
  28→  setIntensity(intensity: "high" | "low" | "pierce" | null): void {
  29→    const texture =
  30→      intensity === "high"
  31→        ? "chen-avoidant"
  32→        : intensity === "low"
  33→          ? "chen-vulnerable"
  34→          : "chen";
  35→    if (this.scene.textures.exists(texture)) {
  36→      this.setTexture(texture);
  37→      this.setScale(this.computeScale());
  38→    }
  39→  }
  40→
  41→  /** 朝向:左/右翻转 */
  42→  face(direction: "left" | "right"): void {
  43→    this.setFlipX(direction === "left");
  44→  }
  45→}
  46→
````

   1→import Phaser from "phaser";
   2→import { ChenSprite } from "../objects/ChenSprite";
   3→
   4→/**
   5→ * 玩家控制器:键盘 A/D + ←→ 移动,E 交互。
   6→ * 发出事件:
   7→ *  - "interact" — 按 E(场景判断是否在 hotspot 范围)
   8→ *  - "submit" — 按 Enter(场景进入抉择)
   9→ */
  10→export class PlayerController {
  11→  public readonly sprite: ChenSprite;
  12→  private cursors: Phaser.Types.Input.Keyboard.CursorKeys;
  13→  private keyA: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;
  14→  private keyD: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;
  15→  private keyE: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;
  16→  private keyEnter: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.Key;
  17→  private speed = 260;
  18→
  19→  constructor(scene: Phaser.Scene, x: number, y: number) {
  20→    this.sprite = new ChenSprite(scene, x, y);
  21→    this.cursors = scene.input.keyboard!.createCursorKeys();
  22→    this.keyA = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey("A");
  23→    this.keyD = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey("D");
  24→    this.keyE = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey("E");
  25→    this.keyEnter = scene.input.keyboard!.addKey("ENTER");
  26→
  27→    this.keyE.on("down", () => scene.events.emit("player:interact"));
  28→    this.keyEnter.on("down", () => scene.events.emit("player:submit"));
  29→  }
  30→
  31→  update() {
  32→    const left = this.cursors.left.isDown || this.keyA.isDown;
  33→    const right = this.cursors.right.isDown || this.keyD.isDown;
  34→
  35→    if (left) {
  36→      this.sprite.setVelocityX(-this.speed);
  37→      this.sprite.face("left");
  38→    } else if (right) {
  39→      this.sprite.setVelocityX(this.speed);
  40→      this.sprite.face("right");
  41→    } else {
  42→      this.sprite.setVelocityX(0);
  43→    }
  44→  }
  45→
  46→  disable() {
  47→    this.sprite.setVelocityX(0);
  48→    this.keyE.enabled = false;
  49→    this.keyEnter.enabled = false;
  50→  }
  51→
  52→  enable() {
  53→    this.keyE.enabled = true;
  54→    this.keyEnter.enabled = true;
  55→  }
  56→}
  57→
````
